name:l‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äçd‚Äça‚Äç_‚Äçy‚Äçu‚Äçn
info:Deluxe Lake-view Twin Room
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:3 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted April 8, 2024
msg:A Disney theme hotel worth visiting twice.
I'll write a small guide by the way, hoping it can help those who want to go later.
Time/Weather:
April 6-7 (the last day of the Qingming Festival and the next working day)
Weather: cloudy on April 6 and light rain on April 7

Day1
1. Immersive experience of the princess entering the castle and exploring the magical world. Fortunately, I upgraded the closet room for free, which is a little surprise that children like. After arriving in the room, I changed my clothes and started the princess's joy.

2. Do small handicrafts in the children's activity room, explore the Hakura Matata Park, and the theme characters will interact intimately from time to time.
Highlights:
Small handicrafts can be taken away, full of Disney elements, and children like it very much.
At 7 o'clock in the evening, I met Gao Fei in the hotel lobby Pluto group photo,
The outdoor lawn is very big and nice. In the evening, when the lights come on, children can have fun.
There will be live performances by a pianist in the lobby from time to time, which creates a good fairytale a**osphere.

2. At 8:15 or 9 pm, you can enjoy the gorgeous fireworks from the rooftop terrace of the hotel, with synchronized sound effects (disadvantages: the distance is a bit far, there is no shock of the scene, and expectations cannot be too high)

3. The hotel has a swimming pool, which is very clean. Those who do not enter the park on the same day can go there to play (we did not bring swimsuits so we skipped it)

4. You can buy limited edition dolls in the hotel fairy shopping center. You get one chance every night you stay. You can choose one of each style. You can only check out at the same time and cannot use them separately (limited edition dolls can only be bought by queuing in the park by lottery, which is a rare opportunity)

5. You don‚Äôt need to buy tickets in advance when staying in the hotel. The hotel can guarantee accommodation Guests can buy tickets for the period of stay, and can buy half-price tickets to enter the park at 3 pm. The real-name system for staying in the hotel is not allowed.

6. The hotel can enjoy an hour early entry to the park, bus transfer/Wishing Lake ferry, round trip is very convenient

Sweetly fall asleep at night, looking forward to starting the next day's park trip...

Tip: The hotel has a buffet, which is a bit expensive. The rich can do it as they please. Ordinary people can take the ferry to Disney Town to stroll around and find food

Day2
Special note: You must get up early and don't sleep in
1. Take the shuttle bus at the hotel entrance at 7 am, take the hotel entrance channel, enjoy early entry, and rush to the projects you want to play as quickly as possible.

2. The projects we have played and route guide:
Dwarf Mine Car-Crazy Zootopia Hot Pursuit (we played it twice in a row, it was great)-The Adventures of Winnie the Pooh-Spinning Crazy Honey Pot-Tomorrowland Flying Machine - (The originally planned Color Celebration Street Party performance was cancelled due to rain) - Immediately changed the reservation to Mickey Mouse Book Tour (a great show) - Mickey Mouse Special Train Parade (Luckily, we came out of the show at about 12:10, just in time to watch the 12:15 parade floats, the kids got into the first row, super happy) - Small town Coucou Hotpot to replenish energy (I would like to praise my companions for being so awesome, I accompanied the little princess to watch the parade floats, and my friends went to Coucou to order some dishes, and after the show we sat down and started eating directly in the restaurant) - After eating, we entered the park and encountered the Color Celebration Party at 2:00 pm (just made up for the Color Celebration that was cancelled in the morning due to rain, and occupied a great position, right opposite the fixed stage, and in the first row. We waited for about 10 minutes, and watched it happily and interactively. The main point was that we were happy and satisfied) - Rope Challenge Course (a bit high and has expansion challenges , Thunder Mountain Rafting is more recommended, but because of the rain, the princesses didn't want to raft and skipped it) - Shipwreck Treasure - Captain Jack (If the time can be stuck, you can go to Jack first, then go to the shipwreck treasure, the route is smoother) - Flying over the horizon - Taking pictures at the big castle (it's time for the princesses to go home, go through the castle to the town, buy gifts at the world store, and take a boat to the hotel to pick up the luggage and go home)

3. In addition:
The Speed ‚Äã‚Äã‚Äã‚ÄãLight Wheel is very fun, but there is a height requirement of 122
The Hug Dragon Sky Racing, the height requirement is 120,

Additional details:
If it rains, the hotel concierge can provide umbrellas that can be taken home, the quality is super good, super considerate

The hotel is not cheap, but for the convenience of the whole play and the experience of the little princesses, it is definitely worth it
For the old mother, only the moment of paying is heartbreaking, and the rest is happiness!

There is a statue of Mickey Mouse when you enter the hotel, as is the elevator in the hotel, and Goofy and Pluto appear in the lobby on the first floor.

The Lumia restaurant in the hotel is very high-end. You can take pictures with Mickey, Minnie, Goofy, and Pluto when you eat at Lumia restaurant. There is no need to queue up to take pictures at the entrance of the restaurant like in Disney. The chef of the restaurant also gave us a piece of rich fish, which was so thoughtful.

The hotel can also buy Disney tickets and give you an exclusive card to choose 1 out of 7. You can also enter the park in advance, and it is very convenient to take the ferry.

The small details in the hotel room are also well done, including a Mickey lamp beside the bed. The waiter's service was also excellent. He looked at me holding my child and carrying my luggage and offered to help me with my luggage.

But the only drawback is that the hotel is not soundproofed. When I lie down and sleep in the room, I can clearly hear the sound of the shower faucet turning on and flushing upstairs or next door.

In short, the advantages outweigh the disadvantages. I am very satisfied with my stay at the Disneyland Hotel. See you next year.

You can enter the park in advance if you stay in the hotel. We chose to enter the park on the day of check-in.
Go out at 7:00 in the morning, check in at the hotel at 7:40, get a temporary room card to store your luggage, then take the hotel bus, and enter the park at 8:10, come back at night and go directly to the room according to the room number notified by the text message.

At the time of purchase, the Disney Hotel did not particularly clearly point out this point. I don't think you can reply me with inexperience, and you are suspected of playing around the corner. Second, the size of the rooms on the executive floor is the same as that of ordinary rooms, which can be seen when booking. Therefore, I think that the administrative building of the Disney Hotel does not feel the trea**ent of the administrative building as a whole. The meals for afternoon tea are also very simple. Therefore, I think the price-to-price ratio of an ordinary room with breakfast included is much higher than that of an administrative building. At night in the administrative building, a Mickey Mouse in pajamas will take a photo with you. There are two Mickey Mouse in the restaurant on the first floor. Compared with Disney's VIP, the fireworks view can only be said to be visible on the seventh floor, and it is very unclear, so it is not the same as seeing it on the spot. It's better to buy another VIP seat for fireworks, it's really worth seeing. Therefore, compared with the ordinary room type, the executive building costs two to three thousand more, and eats a breakfast with much less choices, a limited-time afternoon tea with only desserts, and a limited-time dinner that ends at 7 o'clock with fewer varieties. Is it better to have an ordinary room plus the service experience you can buy with your own money to buy various meals?
